      <script type='text/javascript'>
        //console.log("hash: "+document.location.hash);
        if(document.location.hash && document.location.hash.match(/^#\/\d+\/$/)){
          //console.log("hash match!");
          var pageNumber = document.location.hash.replace(/#/, '');
          //console.log("pageNumber -#: "+pageNumber);
          pageNumber = pageNumber.replace(/\//g, '');
          //console.log("pageNumber -//: "+pageNumber);
          if(pageNumber.match(/^\d+$/)){
            //console.log("pageNumber: "+pageNumber);
            //console.log("InfiniteScroll.starting_url: "+InfiniteScroll.starting_url);
            var pageNumRegex = /\/page\/\d+\//;
            if(InfiniteScroll.starting_url.match(pageNumRegex)){
              var new_location = InfiniteScroll.starting_url.replace(pageNumRegex, "/page/"+pageNumber+"/");
              //console.log("new_location: "+new_location);
            } else {
              var new_location = InfiniteScroll.starting_url.replace(/\/$/, '')+'/page/'+pageNumber+'/';
              //console.log("new_location: "+new_location);
            }
            window.location = new_location;
          }
        }
      </script>
